 Know about 5 such things with which you can maintain your privacy with discipline in office
 1
 Credit to the team: Success-failure in office depends on teamwork
 isliye offis main hameshaa apni hi badai karte rahane se bachein
 You will spoil your own image by making your face melt
 isaki bajaay sabhi ke prayaason kii saraahna karen or positive mindset se rahen
 With this habit, you will win the trust of others and you will not become the center of Gossip
 2
 Avoid Staring: In the office it is often seen that whenever you are typing your personal mail, the colleague sitting next to you looks at your computer carefully or starts reading the mail
 isliye apana privet kaam offis main karne se bachein
 It is wrong if you do it yourself
 apane sahakarmi ke personal chizon ko taakane-jhaankne se dur rahen
 3
 dusron kii bhaawanaaon kii kadra karen:offis main alag-alag kshetron, dharmon or jati se log aate hai
 Therefore, always keep in mind that no one is hurt by your words
 offis main kisi ke dharm or jati ko lekar kuch bhi kehane se bachein
 4
 offis ko gocip adda na banaaen:aap kahin bhi kaam kyon na karen, ho saktaa he ki aap gocip main bad-chadh ke hissaa lete honge yaa iske shikaar ho gaye honge
 If you are involved in office gossip, then think about your personal reputations
 kisi ke bare main galat baaten karke koi olympic medal nahin milane vaala he
 Keep your business and advise others about this
 5
 Use of office phone: Do not do personal things in front of colleagues on the phone as far as possible in the office
 agar aap iske liye offis phone kaa upyog kar rahe hai to yah sabase zyada bura he
 In this way, you will express your secrets to the people sitting around and become the reason for gossip behind

 yah unki majboot chhavi ko kamjor karnaa darsha rahaa tha

 bhale hi upar se ve khud ko purana yogi hone kaa daawa karte rahe

 yah sab 2014 main hone ja rahe loksabhaa chunaavon kii taiyaariyon kaa ek hissaa tha

 LPG prices are determined by the effect of international prices
